(TA.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  You say <foreign lang="ar">مَضَى عَلَيْهِ دَهْرٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">دُهُورٌ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">A long time</hi> and <hi rend="ital">long times,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">an age</hi> and <hi rend="ital">ages,</hi> &amp;c., <hi rend="ital">passed over him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it</hi>].                   <foreign lang="ar">الدَّهْرَ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">He fasted ever,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">always</hi>]. (TA in art. <foreign lang="ar">اول</foreign>, &amp;c. [See a trad. cited voce <foreign lang="ar">آلَ</foreign>, in that art.])          <sense type="b" n="8">-b8-</sense>  [Hence, because, in one sense, time brings to pass events, good and evil,] <foreign lang="ar">الدَّهْرُ</foreign> was applied by the Arabs to <hi rend="ital">Fortune;</hi> or <hi rend="ital">fate:</hi> and they used to blame and revile it: and as the doing so was virtually blaming and reviling God, since events are really brought to pass by Him, Mohammad forbade their doing thus. (Az, Mgh, TA, &amp;c.) It is said in a trad., <foreign lang="ar">لَا تَسُبُّوا ٱلدَّهْرَ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">فَإِنَّ ٱلدَّهْرَ هُوَ ٱللّٰهُ</foreign>, (S, Mgh, TA, &amp;c.,) or, accord. to one reading, <foreign lang="ar">فَإِنَّ ٱللّٰهُ هُوَ ٱلدَّهْرُ</foreign>, (Az, Mgh, TA, &amp;c.,) in which some explain <foreign lang="ar">الدهر</foreign> in the first proposition as having a different meaning from that which it has in the second, whereas others assign to it the same meaning in both cases: (TA:) the meaning of the trad. is, <hi rend="ital">Revile ye not</hi> [<hi rend="ital">fortune,</hi> or] <hi rend="ital">the Efficient of fortune; for the Efficient of fortune is God:</hi> (Az, S, TA, &amp;c.:) or, accord. to the second reading, <hi rend="ital">for God is the Efficient of fortune.</hi> (TA.) Hence, (TA,) some reckon <foreign lang="ar">الدَّهْرُ</foreign> as <hi rend="ital">one of the names of God:</hi> (K, &amp;c.:) but some disallow this: and some say that it is allowable if meant to signify, as rendered above, <hi rend="ital">the Efficient of fortune.</hi> (TA, &amp;c.)          <sense type="b" n="9">-b9-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">زَوْجُ دَهْرٍ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">A husband prepared for the accidents or calamities of fortune.</hi> (S in art. <foreign lang="ar">بهر</foreign>. [See <foreign lang="ar">بَهْرٌ</foreign>.])          <sense type="b" n="10">-b10-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">دَهْرٌ</foreign> also signifies <hi rend="ital">An evil event</hi> or <hi rend="ital">accident; a misfortune; a calamity.</hi> (K.) See also <foreign lang="ar">دَهَارِيرُ</foreign>. [And see 1.]          <sense type="b" n="11">-b11-</sense>  Also <hi rend="ital">A purpose; an intention:</hi> (S, K:) <hi rend="ital">a desire:</hi> (TA:) the <hi rend="ital">scope,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">end that one has in view.</hi> (K, TA.) You say, <foreign lang="ar">مَا دَهْرِى</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">بِكَذَا</foreign>, (S, TA,) and <foreign lang="ar">مَا دَهْرِى كَذَا</foreign>, (TA,) <hi rend="ital">My purpose,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">intention,</hi> (S, TA,) and <hi rend="ital">my desire,</hi> and <hi rend="ital">my scope,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">the end that I have in view,</hi> (TA,) <hi rend="ital">is not such a thing.</hi> (S, TA.)          <sense type="b" n="12">-b12-</sense>  Also <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">A custom,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">habit,</hi> (S, K,) <hi rend="ital">that is constant,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">permanent,</hi> (Kull p. 183,) or <hi rend="ital">that lasts throughout life.</hi> (TA.)
